UUIDv7 provides time-ordered unique IDs. We take the first 8 hex characters,\n901\t/// hash them, and encode as hex for a short, URL-safe identifier.\n902\tpub fn generate_request_id() -> String {\n903\t    let uuid = Uuid::now_v7();\n904\t    let uuid_str = uuid.simple().to_string();\n905\t    // Take first 8 chars (enough entropy for uniqueness)\n906\t    let prefix = &uuid_str[..8];\n907\t\n908\t    // Hash to get a consistent short representation\n909\t    let mut hasher = DefaultHasher::new();\n910\t    prefix.hash(&mut hasher);\n911\t    let hash = hasher.finish();\n912\t\n913\t    // Encode as hex (16 chars = 64 bits)\n914\t    format!(\"{:016x}\", hash)\n915\t}\n916\t\n917\t/// Extension trait to add request ID extraction utilities.\n918\tpub trait RequestIdExt {\n919\t    fn get_request_id(&self) -> Option<String>;\n920\t    fn set_request_id(&mut self, id: &str);\n921\t}\n922\t\n923\timpl RequestIdExt for HeaderMap {\n924\t    fn get_request_id(&self) -> Option<String> {\n925\t        self.get(\"x-request-id\")\n926\t            .and_then(|v| v.to_str().ok())\n927\t            .map(|s| s.to_string())\n928\t    }\n929\t\n930\t    fn set_request_id(&mut self, id: &str) {\n931\t        if let Ok(val) = HeaderValue::from_str(id) {\n932\t            self.insert(\"x-request-id\", val);\n933\t        }\n934\t    }\n935\t}\n936\t\n937\t/// Guard that decrements the in-flight gauge when dropped.\n938\t///\n939\t/// This ensures that even if the handler panics, the in-flight count\n940\t/// is accurately decremented.\n941\tstruct InFlightGuard {\n942\t    metrics: Metrics,\n943\t    request_id: String,\n944\t}\n945\t\n946\timpl InFlightGuard {\n947\t    fn new(metrics: Metrics, request_id: String) -> Self {\n948\t        metrics.requests_in_flight.inc();\n949\t        tracing::trace!(\n950\t            request_id = %request_id,\n951\t            requests_in_flight = metrics.requests_in_flight.get(),\n952\t            \"request started\"\n953\t        );\n954\t        Self { metrics, request_id }\n955\t    }\n956\t}\n957\t\n958\timpl Drop for InFlightGuard {\n959\t    fn drop(&mut self) {\n960\t        self.metrics.requests_in_flight.dec();\n961\t        tracing::trace!(\n962\t            request_id = %self.request_id,\n963\t            requests_in_flight = self.metrics.requests_in_flight.get(),\n964\t            \"request completed\"\n965\t        );\n966\t    }\n967\t}\n968\t\n969\t/// Extract the path template from the matched route.\n970\t///\n971\t/// Axum's MatchedPath extractor provides the route template (e.g., \"/indexes/{uid}/search\")\n972\t/// instead of the actual path (e.g., \"/indexes/products/search\"), avoiding high-cardinality labels.\n973\tfn extract_path_template(request: &Request) -> String {\n974\t    request\n975\t        .extensions()\n976\t        .get::<axum::extract::MatchedPath>()\n977\t        .map(|mp| mp.as_str())\n978\t        .unwrap_or_else(|| request.uri().path())\n979\t        .to_string()\n980\t}\n981\t\n982\t/// Main middleware that combines request ID injection, structured logging, and Prometheus metrics.\n983\t///\n984\t/// IMPORTANT: This middleware must be applied AFTER request_id_middleware in the layer stack\n985\t/// (i.e., its layer() call must come BEFORE request_id_middleware's layer() call).\n986\t/// This ensures the request_id header is already set when this middleware runs.\n987\tpub async fn telemetry_middleware(\n988\t    State(telemetry): State<TelemetryState>,\n989\t    mut req: Request,\n990\t    next: Next,\n991\t) -> Response {\n992\t    let start = Instant::now();\n993\t    let method = req.method().clone();\n994\t    let path_template = extract_path_template(&req);\n995\t    let metrics = telemetry.metrics.clone();\n996\t    let pod_id = telemetry.pod_id.clone();\n997\t\n998\t    // Extract request ID from header (set by request_id_middleware)\n999\t    // The header must already exist because request_id_middleware runs first.\n1000\t    let request_id = req\n1001\t        .headers()\n1002\t        .get_request_id()\n1003\t        .expect(\"request_id header must be set by request_id_middleware\");\n1004\t    req.headers_mut().set_request_id(&request_id);\n1005\t\n1006\t    // Create span for structured logging with pod_id included.\n1007\t    // Note: raw path is intentionally omitted to avoid logging index names\n1008\t    // (which may contain customer identifiers). Use path_template instead.\n1009\t    let span = info_span!(\n1010\t        \"request\",\n1011\t        request_id = %request_id,\n1012\t        pod_id = %pod_id,\n1013\t        method = %method,\n1014\t        path_template = %path_template,\n1015\t    );\n1016\t\n1017\t    let _guard = span.enter();\n1018\t\n1019\t    // Track in-flight requests\n1020\t    let in_flight = InFlightGuard::new(metrics.clone(), request_id.clone());\n1021\t\n1022\t    let response = next.run(req).await;\n1023\t\n1024\t    drop(in_flight);\n1025\t\n1026\t    let status = response.status();\n1027\t    let status_u16 = status.as_u16();\n1028\t    let duration = start.elapsed();\n1029\t\n1030\t    // Record Prometheus metrics\n1031\t    metrics\n1032\t        .request_duration\n1033\t        .with_label_values(&[method.as_str(), &path_template, &status_u16.to_string()])\n1034\t        .observe(duration.as_secs_f64());\n1035\t    metrics\n1036\t        .requests_total\n1037\t        .with_label_values(&[method.as_str(), &path_template, &status_u16.to_string()])\n1038\t        .inc();\n1039\t\n1040\t    // Structured log entry (plan §10 shape)\n1041\t    // Base fields: timestamp (from tracing-subscriber), level, message, duration_ms\n1042\t    // Additional fields (index, node_count, estimated_hits, degraded)\n1043\t    // are added by request handlers via the tracing span.\n1044\t    let message = format!(\"{} {}\", method, status);\n1045\t    if status.is_server_error() {\n1046\t        tracing::error!(\n1047\t            target: \"miroir.request\",\n1048\t            pod_id = %pod_id,\n1049\t            request_id = %request_id,\n1050\t            message = %message,\n1051\t            duration_ms = duration.as_millis() as u64,\n1052\t            status = status_u16,\n1053\t            method = %method,\n1054\t            path_template = %path_template,\n1055\t        );\n1056\t    } else if status.is_client_error() {\n1057\t        tracing::warn!(\n1058\t            target: \"miroir.request\",\n1059\t            pod_id = %pod_id,\n1060\t            request_id = %request_id,\n1061\t            message = %message,\n1062\t            duration_ms = duration.as_millis() as u64,\n1063\t            status = status_u16,\n1064\t            method = %method,\n1065\t            path_template = %path_template,\n1066\t        );\n1067\t    } else {\n1068\t        tracing::info!(\n1069\t            target: \"miroir.request\",\n1070\t            pod_id = %pod_id,\n1071\t            request_id = %request_id,\n1072\t            message = %message,\n1073\t            duration_ms = duration.as_millis() as u64,\n1074\t            status = status_u16,\n1075\t            method = %method,\n1076\t            path_template = %path_template,\n1077\t        );\n1078\t    }\n1079\t\n1080\t    // Ensure request ID is in response headers\n1081\t    let mut response = response;\n1082\t    if !response.headers().contains_key(\"x-request-id\") {\n1083\t        if let Ok(val) = HeaderValue::from_str(&request_id) {\n1084\t            response.headers_mut().insert(\"x-request-id\", val);\n1085\t        }\n1086\t    }\n1087\t\n1088\t    response\n1089\t}\n1090\t\n1091\t/// Create the metrics router for the :9090 server.\n1092\tpub fn metrics_router() -> Router<Metrics> {\n1093\t    Router::new().route(\"/metrics\", get(metrics_handler))\n1094\t}\n1095\t\n1096\t/// Handler that returns Prometheus metrics in text exposition format.\n1097\tasync fn metrics_handler(State(metrics): State<Metrics>) -> String {\n1098\t    match metrics.encode_metrics() {\n1099\t        Ok(metrics) => metrics,\n1100\t        Err(e) => {\n1101\t            tracing::error!(error = %e, \"failed to encode metrics\");\n1102\t            format!(\"# ERROR: failed to encode metrics: {}\\n\", e)\n1103\t        }\n1104\t    }\n1105\t}\n1106\t\n1107\t/// Accessor methods for metrics that can be used }\n1500\t}\n1501\t\n1502\t#[cfg(test)]\n1503\tmod tests {\n1504\t    use super::*;\n1505\t\n1506\t    #[test]\n1507\t    fn test_request_id_generation() {\n1508\t        // Generate multiple IDs to original HTTP status code from\n175\t    /// the node response rather than deriving it from the error type.\n176\t    pub fn forwarded(json: &str) -> Option<Self> {\n177\t raw.message,\n189\t            code: raw.code,\n190\t            error_type: raw.error_type,\n191\t            link: raw.link,\n192\t        })\n193\t    }\n194\t\n195\t    /// Derive the HTTP status http_status(&self) -> u16 {\n200\t        MiroirCode::from_code_str(&self.code)\n201\t            .map(|c| c.http_status())\n202\t            .unwrap_or_else(|| match self.error_type {\n203\t                ErrorType::InvalidRequest => 400,\n204\t                ErrorType::Auth => 401,\n205\t                ErrorType::Internal => 500,\n206\t                ErrorType::System => 503,\n207\t            })\n208\t    }\n209\t}\n210\t\n211\t#[cfg(feature = \"axum\")]\n212\timpl IntoResponse for MeilisearchError {\n213\t    fn into_response(self) -> Response {\n214\t        let status = .into_response()\n226\t    }\n227\t}\n228\t\n229\t#[cfg(test)]\n230\tmod tests {\n231\t    use super::*;\n232\t\n233\t    // -- Per-code JSON shape tests Meilisearch-compatible API error shape and Miroir-specific error codes.\n//!\n//! All errors use the Meilisearch error shape:\n//! ```json\n//! {\"message\": \"...\", \"code\": \"...\", \"type\": \"invalid_request\", \"link\": \"...\"}\n//! ```\n//!\n//! Miroir-specific codes live under the `miroir_` prefix so that existing\n//! Meilisearch SDKs' \"unknown error\" branches handle them safely.\n\nuse serde::Serialize;\n\n#[cfg(feature = \"axum\")]\nuse axum::{http::{StatusCode, header}, response::{IntoResponse, Response}};\n\n/// Error type categories matching Meilisearch's classification.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = \"snake_case\")]\npub enum ErrorType {\n    InvalidRequest,\n    Auth,\n    Internal,\n    System,\n}\n\n/// Miroir-specific error codes with associated metadata.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub enum MiroirCode {\n    PrimaryKeyRequired,\n    NoQuorum,\n    ShardUnavailable,\n    ReservedField,\n    IdempotencyKeyReused,\n    SettingsVersionStale,\n    MultiAliasNotWritable,\n    JwtInvalid,\n    JwtScopeDenied,\n    InvalidAuth,\n    MissingCsrf,\n    CsrfMismatch,\n    IndexAlreadyExists,\n    Timeout,\n}\n\nimpl MiroirCode {\n    /// All variants, used for iteration in tests.\n    #[cfg(test)]\n    const ALL: [MiroirCode; 14] = [\n        MiroirCode::PrimaryKeyRequired,\n        MiroirCode::NoQuorum,\n        MiroirCode::ShardUnavailable,\n        MiroirCode::ReservedField,\n        MiroirCode::IdempotencyKeyReused,\n        MiroirCode::SettingsVersionStale,\n        MiroirCode::MultiAliasNotWritable,\n        MiroirCode::JwtInvalid,\n        MiroirCode::JwtScopeDenied,\n        MiroirCode::InvalidAuth,\n        MiroirCode::MissingCsrf,\n        MiroirCode::CsrfMismatch,\n        MiroirCode::IndexAlreadyExists,\n        MiroirCode::Timeout,\n    ];\n\n    /// Returns the error code string (e.g., `\"miroir_no_quorum\"`).\n    pub fn as_str(&self) -> &'static str {\n        match self {\n            Self::PrimaryKeyRequired => \"miroir_primary_key_required\",\n            Self::NoQuorum => \"miroir_no_quorum\",\n            Self::ShardUnavailable => \"miroir_shard_unavailable\",\n            Self::ReservedField => \"miroir_reserved_field\",\n            Self::IdempotencyKeyReused => \"miroir_idempotency_key_reused\",\n            Self::SettingsVersionStale => \"miroir_settings_version_stale\",\n            Self::MultiAliasNotWritable => \"miroir_multi_alias_not_writable\",\n            Self::JwtInvalid => \"miroir_jwt_invalid\",\n            Self::JwtScopeDenied => \"miroir_jwt_scope_denied\",\n            Self::InvalidAuth => \"miroir_invalid_auth\",\n            Self::MissingCsrf => \"miroir_missing_csrf\",\n            Self::CsrfMismatch => \"miroir_csrf_mismatch\",\n            Self::IndexAlreadyExists => \"miroir_index_already_exists\",\n            Self::Timeout => \"miroir_timeout\",\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Returns the Meilisearch-compatible error type category.\n    pub fn error_type(&self) -> ErrorType {\n        match self {\n            Self::PrimaryKeyRequired\n            | Self::ReservedField\n            | Self::IdempotencyKeyReused\n            | Self::MultiAliasNotWritable\n            | Self::IndexAlreadyExists => ErrorType::InvalidRequest,\n\n            Self::JwtInvalid | Self::JwtScopeDenied | Self::InvalidAuth | Self::MissingCsrf | Self::CsrfMismatch => ErrorType::Auth,\n\n            Self::NoQuorum | Self::ShardUnavailable | Self::SettingsVersionStale | Self::Timeout => {\n                ErrorType::System\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Returns the HTTP status code for this error.\n    pub fn http_status(&self) -> u16 {\n        match self {\n            Self::PrimaryKeyRequired | Self::ReservedField => 400,\n            Self::JwtInvalid | Self::InvalidAuth | Self::MissingCsrf => 401,\n            Self::JwtScopeDenied | Self::CsrfMismatch => 403,\n            Self::IdempotencyKeyReused | Self::MultiAliasNotWritable => 409,\n            Self::IndexAlreadyExists => 409,\n            Self::Timeout => 504,\n            Self::NoQuorum | Self::ShardUnavailable | Self::SettingsVersionStale => 503,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Generates the documentation link for this error code.\n    pub fn doc_link(&self) -> String {\n        format!(\n            \"https://github.com/jedarden/miroir/blob/main/docs/errors.md#{}\",\n            self.as_str()\n        )\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a code string back to a [`MiroirCode`].\n    pub fn from_code_str(s: &str) -> Option<Self> {\n        match s {\n            \"miroir_primary_key_required\" => Some(Self::PrimaryKeyRequired),\n            \"miroir_no_quorum\" => Some(Self::NoQuorum),\n            \"miroir_shard_unavailable\" => Some(Self::ShardUnavailable),\n            \"miroir_reserved_field\" => Some(Self::ReservedField),\n            \"miroir_idempotency_key_reused\" => Some(Self::IdempotencyKeyReused),\n            \"miroir_settings_version_stale\" => Some(Self::SettingsVersionStale),\n            \"miroir_multi_alias_not_writable\" => Some(Self::MultiAliasNotWritable),\n            \"miroir_jwt_invalid\" => Some(Self::JwtInvalid),\n            \"miroir_jwt_scope_denied\" => Some(Self::JwtScopeDenied),\n            \"miroir_invalid_auth\" => Some(Self::InvalidAuth),\n            \"miroir_missing_csrf\" => Some(Self::MissingCsrf),\n            \"miroir_csrf_mismatch\" => Some(Self::CsrfMismatch),\n            \"miroir_index_already_exists\" => Some(Self::IndexAlreadyExists),\n            \"miroir_timeout\" => Some(Self::Timeout),\n            _ => None,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Meilisearch-compatible error response shape.\n///\n/// Both Miroir-specific and forwarded Meilisearch-native errors use this shape\n/// so that existing SDK error handling branches remain functional.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, thiserror::Error, Serialize)]\n#[error(\"{message}\")]\npub struct MeilisearchError {\n    pub message: String,\n    pub code: String,\n    #[serde(rename = \"type\")]\n    pub error_type: ErrorType,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub link: Option<String>,\n}\n\nimpl MeilisearchError {\n    /// Create a new miroir-specific error with auto-generated doc link.\n    pub fn new(code: MiroirCode, message: impl Into<String>) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            message: message.into(),\n            code: code.as_str().to_string(),\n            error_type: code.error_type(),\n            link: Some(code.doc_link()),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Create from a forwarded Meilisearch node error response body.\n    ///\n    /// Returns `None` if the body cannot be parsed as a Meilisearch error shape.\n    /// When forwarding, the caller should use the original HTTP status code from\n    /// the node response rather than deriving it from the error type.\n    pub fn forwarded(json: &str) -> Option<Self> {\n        #[derive(serde::Deserialize)]\n        struct Raw {\n            message: String,\n            code: String,\n            #[serde(rename = \"type\")]\n            error_type: ErrorType,\n            link: Option<String>,\n        }\n\n        let raw: Raw = serde_json::from_str(json).ok()?;\n        Some(Self {\n            message: raw.message,\n            code: raw.code,\n            error_type: raw.error_type,\n            link: raw.link,\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Derive the HTTP status code for a miroir-generated error.\n    ///\n    /// For forwarded Meilisearch errors, prefer using the original node HTTP\n    /// status code instead.\n    pub fn http_status(&self) -> u16 {\n        MiroirCode::from_code_str(&self.code)\n            .map(|c| c.http_status())\n            .unwrap_or_else(|| match self.error_type {\n                ErrorType::InvalidRequest => 400,\n                ErrorType::Auth => 401,\n                ErrorType::Internal => 500,\n                ErrorType::System => 503,\n            })\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(feature = \"axum\")]\nimpl IntoResponse for MeilisearchError {\n    fn into_response(self) -> Response {\n        let status = self.http_status();\n\n        let body = serde_json::to_string(&self).unwrap_or_else(|_| {\n            r#\"{\"message\":\"internal error\",\"code\":\"internal\",\"type\":\"internal\"}\"#.to_string()\n        });\n\n        (\n            StatusCode::from_u16(status).unwrap_or(StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR),\n            [(header::CONTENT_TYPE, \"application/json\")],\n            body,\n        )\n            .into_response()\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    // -- Per-code JSON shape tests ------------------------------------------------\n\n    #[test]\n    fn miroir_primary_key_required_shape()
